\DoxyCodeLine{62         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH ) \textcolor{keyword}{noexcept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{64         TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{65         TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{66         Width = width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{67         Height = height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{68         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{69         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{70     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71     \textcolor{keyword}{explicit} CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT(}
\DoxyCodeLine{72         \_In\_ ID3D12Resource* pResource,}
\DoxyCodeLine{73         UINT mipSlice = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{74         FLOAT topLeftX = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{75         FLOAT topLeftY = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{76         FLOAT minDepth = D3D12\_MIN\_DEPTH,}
\DoxyCodeLine{77         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH ) \textcolor{keyword}{noexcept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{79         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} Desc = pResource-\/>GetDesc();}
\DoxyCodeLine{80         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceWidth = Desc.Width >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{81         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceHeight = Desc.Height >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{82         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (Desc.Dimension)}
\DoxyCodeLine{83         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{84         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_BUFFER:}
\DoxyCodeLine{85             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{86             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{87             Width = float(Desc.Width) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{88             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{89             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{90         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE1D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{91             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{92             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{93             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? float(SubresourceWidth) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{94             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{95             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{96         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE2D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{97         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE3D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{98             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{99             TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{100             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? float(SubresourceWidth) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{101             Height = (SubresourceHeight ? float(SubresourceHeight) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{102             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{103         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{104         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 }
\DoxyCodeLine{106         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{107         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{108     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{3309 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310 \textcolor{comment}{// D3DX12 State Object Creation Helpers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3312 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper classes for creating new style state objects out of an arbitrary set of subobjects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3313 \textcolor{comment}{// Uses STL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3314 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315 \textcolor{comment}{// Start by instantiating CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC (see it's public methods).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316 \textcolor{comment}{// One of its methods is CreateSubobject(), which has a comment showing a couple of options for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317 \textcolor{comment}{// defining subobjects using the helper classes for each subobject (CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3318 \textcolor{comment}{// etc.). The subobject helpers each have methods specific to the subobject for configuring it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3319 \textcolor{comment}{// contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3320 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3321 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3382     \textcolor{comment}{// CreateSubobject creates a sububject helper (e.g. CD3DX12\_HIT\_GROUP\_SUBOBJECT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3383     \textcolor{comment}{// whose lifetime is owned by this class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3384     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3385     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3386     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC Collection1(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_COLLECTION);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3387     \textcolor{comment}{//    auto Lib0 = Collection1.CreateSubobject<CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT>();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3388     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[0]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3389     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>DefineExport(L"{}rayGenShader0"{}); // in practice these export listings might be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3390     \textcolor{comment}{//                                          // data/engine driven}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3391     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3392     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393     \textcolor{comment}{// Alternatively, users can instantiate sububject helpers explicitly, such as via local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394     \textcolor{comment}{// variables instead, passing the state object desc that should point to it into the helper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395     \textcolor{comment}{// constructor (or call mySubobjectHelper.AddToStateObject(Collection1)).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3396     \textcolor{comment}{// In this alternative scenario, the user must keep the subobject alive as long as the state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397     \textcolor{comment}{// object it is associated with is alive, else it's pointer references will be stale.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3398     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3399     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC RaytracingState2(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_RAYTRACING\_PIPELINE);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT LibA(RaytracingState2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402     \textcolor{comment}{//    LibA.SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[4]); // not manually specifying exports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // -\/ meaning all exports in the libraries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3404     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // are exported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3406 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3407     \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
